     <section class="section swatch-white billie_holiday_back section-text-no-shadow section-inner-no-shadow section-normal section-opaque" data-label="">
      <div class="background-overlay grid-overlay-0 " style="background-color: rgba(0,0,0,0);">

       <div class="row vertical-middle">
        <div class="col-md-6 text-default small-screen-default">

         <div class=" element-short-top element-short-bottom" data-os-animation="none" data-os-animation-delay="0s">
          <h1>
           Captain’s apartments hotel in Corfu Barbati
          </h1>
          <p>
           Captain’s apartment Hotel is situated in Barbati, one of the most picturesque areas of the north east coast of Corfu, an island where the past and future intertwine and whose charm comes from its hospitable inhabitants.
          </p>
          <p>
           Catering for the needs of our guests for over 23 years now and guided by the saying “Your wishes are our commands”, it is our pleasure to attend to your every need and make your stay in Captain’s apartments Hotel a memorable one.
          </p>
          <p>
           Irini the owner of Captain’s, lives in the complex, and is always available to help you and make your stay comfortable.
          </p>

         <div class=" element-short-top element-short-bottom" data-os-animation="none" data-os-animation-delay="0s">
          <h2>
           About us
          </h2>
          <p>
           Captain’s apartments Hotel has been offering its clients a friendly family atmosphere since 1990. The concept of Captain’s apartments Hotel is to offer impeccable service, where guests feel relaxed, just like at home! Our Hotel is comprised of 16 spacious accommodation self-catering units/apartments fully equipped with all the comforts one would expect, with private terraces or balconies offering a unique panoramic view over the clear blue Ionian Sea or the luscious green countryside.
          </p>
          <p>
           At our swimming pool area and relaxing hillside terrace you will enjoy your morning breakfast, refreshing drinks, snacks, meals, spectacular sea views over the Barbati bay up to Corfu town in the distance and, most importantly, a great holiday atmosphere! In our hotel you will find all services and amenities for an impeccable stay.
          </p>
          <p>
           There is a frequent green bus service from Corfu Town to Barbati. The bus stops just 50 meters from the hotel. To get to Captain’s Barbati apartments and studios by car from the airport, follow the signs to Corfu Port. From there keep following signs to Kassiopi, always keeping the sea at your right hand side.When you reach Barbati drive almost to the end of the village and you will find Captain’s at your left hand side
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="divider-wrapper" style="visibility:hidden;background-color:">
          <div class="visible-xs" style="height:24px;">
          </div>
          <div class="visible-sm" style="height:24px;">
          </div>
          <div class="visible-md" style="height:35px;">
          </div>
          <div class="visible-lg" style="height:45px;">
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
